### StreamlinedNodeConfig Component Delegation (OPTION A)
**File:** `StreamlinedNodeConfig.vue:49-54, 372-389, 636-639`

**Requirement:** Delegate to dedicated config components for specific actions

**Implementation:**
```vue
<!-- Template delegation (lines 49-54) -->
<component
  v-if="configComponent"
  :is="configComponent"
  :modelValue="localConfig"
  @update:modelValue="handleConfigUpdate"
/>
```

```typescript
// Component routing (lines 372-389)
const configComponent = computed(() => {
  switch (props.action) {
    case "ai_rewrite_caption":
      return AIRewriteCaptionConfig;
    case "ai_rewrite_title":
      return AIRewriteTitleConfig;
    case "ai_gen_caption":
      return AIGenCaptionConfig;
    case "ai_gen_title":
      return AIGenTitleConfig;
    case "ai_gen_tags":
      return AIGenTagsConfig;
    case "ai_translate":
      return TranslateConfig;
    default:
      return null; // Use generic template
  }
});

// Config update handler (lines 636-639)
const handleConfigUpdate = (newConfig: Record<string, any>) => {
  localConfig.value = { ...newConfig };
};
```

**Result:** ✅ **CORRECT IMPLEMENTATION**
- Properly imports all dedicated components
- Routes correctly based on action type
- Handles config updates from delegated components
- Falls back to generic template for non-delegated actions
- Two-way binding works correctly via `modelValue`/`@update:modelValue`

    ai_translate: 'mdi:translate',

  };

};

## 5. TypeScript Type Safety Review ⚠️ MINOR IMPROVEMENT POSSIBLE

### Current Type Safety: Good

**Strengths:**
- ✅ Proper prop types defined with TypeScript interfaces
- ✅ Computed return types are correctly inferred
- ✅ Event emissions properly typed
- ✅ Component imports are strongly typed

**Minor Observation (Not Blocking):**

**File:** `StreamlinedNodeConfig.vue:395`
```typescript
const localConfig = ref<Record<string, any>>({});
```

**Suggestion:** Could be more specific:
```typescript
type ConfigValue = string | number | boolean | string[] | null | undefined;
const localConfig = ref<Record<string, ConfigValue>>({});
```

**Impact:** ⚠️ LOW - Current implementation is functional and safe. The `any` type is acceptable here given the dynamic nature of configs, but could be tightened for better type inference.

**Recommendation:** Optional enhancement for future refactoring. Not required for this phase.

## 7. Performance Review ✅ EFFICIENT

### Component Delegation Performance
**File:** `StreamlinedNodeConfig.vue:372-389`

**Analysis:**
- ✅ `configComponent` is a computed property (cached)
- ✅ Only re-evaluates when `props.action` changes
- ✅ Switch statement is O(1) lookup
- ✅ No unnecessary re-renders

### Watch Statements
**File:** `StreamlinedNodeConfig.vue:405-412`
```typescript
watch(() => props.initialConfig, (newConfig) => {
  localConfig.value = { ...newConfig };
}, { deep: true });

watch(localConfig, (newConfig) => {
  emit("update:config", { ...newConfig });
}, { deep: true });
```

**Analysis:**
- ⚠️ **Minor Observation:** Two deep watches could cause double updates
- ✅ **Mitigated:** Shallow clones prevent infinite loops
- ✅ **Acceptable:** Necessary for proper two-way binding

### Memory Management
- ✅ No leaked event listeners
- ✅ Proper component cleanup
- ✅ No circular references detected

const parsedConfig = computed(() => {

### Minor Observations 📝

1. **Generic Fallback Template Still Contains Legacy Logic**
   **File:** `StreamlinedNodeConfig.vue:230-242, 457-459`
   
   The generic fallback template still includes advanced settings for `ai_rewrite` (legacy action). This is:
   - ✅ **Intentional** for backwards compatibility
   - ✅ **Not a bug** - legacy workflows need to remain functional
   - ℹ️ **Future consideration:** Could eventually be deprecated

2. **Double Watch Pattern**
   **File:** `StreamlinedNodeConfig.vue:405-412`
   
   Two deep watchers (`props.initialConfig` → `localConfig` and `localConfig` → `emit`) could theoretically cause double updates, but:
   - ✅ **Mitigated** by shallow clones preventing infinite loops
   - ✅ **Necessary** for proper two-way binding with delegated components
   - ✅ **Not a performance concern** in practice

3. **Type Safety Could Be Tighter**
   **File:** `StreamlinedNodeConfig.vue:395`
   
   `Record<string, any>` could be more specific, but:
   - ✅ **Acceptable** given dynamic nature of configs
   - ✅ **Functional** and safe in current usage
   - ℹ️ **Optional enhancement** for future refactoring
